Didn't blink,  so much to see. Big smile as I reminisced treats of my childhood, and discovered items new to me and my grandson.  I could spend a cool hour here just looking through everything.  It was all giggles and smiles until check out.  A middle aged male didn't bother to pause his personal call on his cell to say hello, seemed displeased that we were disrupting his call.  I thought perhaps it was bad news because I noticed him on his phone when we walked in being the only customers in the store at the time.  Based on his stoic face, I decided to give the poor guy a break, until he stated laughing like a school girl then returned to his previous flat face conversation.  I wish I spoke his native tongue so I could interrupt his conversation to say, HELLO I'M HAPPY YOU'RE NOT HAVING A BAD DAY. He continued to ignor us as he rang up items, only made eye contact to accept payment which was via debit card then he directed me by pointing out a chip reader. No bag offered for the multiple lil items purchased, no goodbye,  ZIP and my first and last visit was over.  Too bad as I would have happily made this a reward center for my grandson. Hope you all have better luck with customer service then we had.  Gave 4 stars because of the store concept would have given 5 stars for even bland customer service.< /review>

<review>Very small establishment, but the ramen specifically is well worth the money you will spend there. They have inside seating and outside seating. The pork (chasu) is so juicy and flavorful, it's the best chasu in ramen that I've tasted in the area. The red ramen (what I ordered) isnt overly spicy and could be considered mild but its a massive serving and very tasty.

I also ordered the gyoza, and although the gyoza itself tasted decent (not the best) the sauce served with it didnt really taste good to me.

All in all, big serving, tasty and flavorful ramen with chasu is highly recommended, the only reason it's 4 stars instead of 5 is because of the mildness of the ramen and the sauce served with the gyoza.< /review><pics>None</pics><response>None</response>< GmapID>

< Review>
Still more or less in shock at this find of a restaurant. If you blink, you would miss it walking by. Nothing in the area suggests that a top-tier ramen restaurant would be nestled in a strip mall. My coworkers and I got the poke and red ramen bowls. The broth here beats most locations in downtown LA. Portions are, in a word, large. The poke bowl offers vegetable noodles, which is a refreshing option for those looking to avoid carbs. Quick wait time and overall incredible experience.</Review>

<username>Recruit Mattix Sifuentes< /username>< Time>
1381074388399</Time>
<rating>3< /rating><text>It is tucked away and hidden behind an industrial area of La Mirada. It is located about 1 mile from the Santa Fe Springs Swap Meet and 1 mile from Neff Park. This is not like your typical railway museum but it's a nice spot to spend a few minutes of your time entertaining any child who finds trains to be exciting. I do not recommend pulling into the yard because it is a work site. However, you can pull into an adjacent parking lot that positions you safely and just right where your family can watch different rail cars pass. You will see freight and passenger cars pass through here every few minutes. Occasionally, you might see the coupling of train cars if your lucky. It is free which is great if your on a budget and looking for something to excite your kids.

After visiting this spot I recommend you visit Neff Park, which is about 1 mile away where your kids can run and play and still see and hear passing train cars from a distance.

I gave this a 3 star rating because it doesn't provide any hands on interaction for the kids but it's still a viable option depending on your family's preference.</text><pics>None<//pics>< resp>

<user_name>Catherine Morton<//user_name><Date>1551512263435< /Date>< Rate>
5<//Rate>
< text>
I was part of a group that enjoyed an evening  at Frank Sinatra‚Äôs estate hosted by a very talented Frank Sinatra impersonator. We had dinner on the lawn by the pool while the pianist played inside.   After dinner, we gathered in the living room.  Mr.  Sinatra entertained us with popular ballads. The home was lit up and inviting. Hosts shared details about each room and told stories about things that happened back in the day. The mid-century modern home made it feel like we stepped back in time to get a glimpse of what it may have been like going to a dinner party hosted by Frank Sinatra in his own home.  I highly recommend this venue and the group that hosted the event. They were attentive and welcoming.  Dinner was a bit over cooked but the atmosphere and ambience more than made up for the chewy steak and dry salmon.  It was a unique experience that I will never forget.</text>

<username>Lawrence Moxley< /username><Date>1601096611518<//Date><Rate>3< /Rate>< Text>
the ultimate ice cream experience.

I rarely go for ice cream since it's on the less healthy side of food or desert choices. I regard it as a slow heart attack item.

Nevertheless, gotta go sometime.

Meaning, when in particular company, icecream is a nice added feature presenting cool social benefits.

I mean you can't not share a sample with your date or companion.

Anyway, the cold stone gimmick of mashing and mixing the icecream on the cold stone slab adds to the entertainment of the moment.

And the waffle layout in a dish makes for a total yum experience.

Even if it adds to clogging of arteries and a quicker route to six feet under.<//Text>

< review>
After a long Saturday on Venice Beach Boardwalk, we decided to take a short 12 min walk to Cabo Cantina for dinner. The walk was stunning! Glass houses to the left,  the sun setting on the beach to the right. Security checked our ID and we were on our own to find seating. All 3 levels were packed to capacity, which were a little discouraging, but we were able to squeeze two stool seats to the fire pit bar for a very beautiful scenic dinner setting. I had to go grab food menus from the back bar, and we waited about 10 mins before a waitress found us to take our order. The music was blaring some of our favorite 90‚Äôa jams, so the wait didn‚Äôt seem long. The wings that I once ordered at the Hollywood location weren‚Äôt on the menu, so I ordered the  chicken sunset rolls with a side of fries and Ari ordered the queso dip (with added shrimp). We shared a raspberry margarita. The sunset rolls melted in my mouth, um um good. The fries were fresh and hot thick wedged. Ari‚Äôs queso dip looked like mush and she said it turned her stomach. The margarita was ‚Äúok‚Äù in taste to me, but Ari said it tasted like medicine. I liked the loud environment, Ari said she didn‚Äôt like the people dancing so close to where we ate. 3.5 stars because booth parties should love the venue for 5 stars. I rounded up to 4 stars because I personally liked this place a lot to finish a fun Beach day.< /review>

<Rate>1</Rate><Text>PLEASE! Read your RECEIPT!!

This is coming from a customer who has been to this and MANY Cabo Cantina's and I believe they are trained to skim (not scam) the customers.

They literally take your order with a smile, then serve you whatever drink they want. OR They serve you what you order and add El DORADO to the bill. El Dorado is the premium drink that is $12.95 or $13.95 depending on how they decide to bill it (or their fancy keying or renaming it to another, cheaper drink). I ALWAYS order the TJ classic which is $7.95 and the most basic Jose Cuervo Margarita.

They will charge for the El Dorado (Patron tequila) margarita and say they made a mistake if you challenge it. Then, instead of changing that, they offer to remove a food item (for alcohol billing and for skimming purposes) instead of adjusting the real price of the drinks you ORDERED.  They will say the price difference (b/c its not listed on the menu) is only $1 or $2 but as you can see, its $5 or $6!

In the End, ALWAYS check your receipt.  Do NOT pay for drinks misattributed to your bill. And, do NOT let them take advantage of you, because as long as I have been going there, THEY WILL ALWAYS TRY!.

I have been going there for over 11 years, and Everytime, EVERY location, they try the same skim (scam) and everytime I catch them, call them out, and get my bill adjusted!

Do the SAME!</Text>< Pics>

<rating>3</rating><Text>If you are looking for a place to drink next to the beach with less than ridiculous pricing, than this is a decent option. Well, pretty good considering it's one of only a few options.

Their margaritas are insanely sweet, even the classic. Also, please note that pricing on drinks can be a bit deceptive, especially during happy hour.

Food on the other hand is surprisingly good. Flavorful and in pretty generous portions, this is definitely not a good place for a diet but great with a beer or two.

Service is pretty unresponsive, so it isn't a great place if you're in a rush. But if you're afternoon or evening is relaxed, it's not a bad place to spend some time.</Text>< pictures>

Extremely racist! We came in with a group of college educated, professional people after a HBCU event and the manager immediately got concerned. He walked over to us as we were walking in and said, "we don't want any loud noise in here." "What?", I thought in my head. What insinuated that we were going to be loud? Outside of you judging the color of our skin. After all we are at a bar not a quiet, fancy restaurant. It was filled with white people talking loud, singing and having a good time. Yet as soon as we walked in we were asked or told not to be loud. We hadn't even taken our seats yet. As the time went on we were met with extremely poor service. The waitress took 15-20 mins before she ever arrived to our table, got our orders incorrect and demanded that we pay first. It's our policy she exclaimed. Not true by they way. Our food never came out and the manager kept walking by watching everything we were doing. One my friends heard something funny and busted out laughing and slapped the table in a big chuckle. The manager approached us and said we can't make noise or slap the table and asked us to leave. We willing complied because we were done with the rude treatment and politely asked for our credit cards back and a refund on the food we never received because we were still waiting on it to arrive. The manager said to an employee "they just don't want to pay for their food." How is that so when we paid in advance for the food? The food was never delivered to us (purposely). <time>1415834348696<//time>< rating>
4</rating>
<text>For several years now I've been coming to this Cabo Cantina every so often. Mostly to watch sports and have some of their giant margaritas. I finally went to their Taco Tuesday and I was very impressed!

I've never liked their food much (I'm Mexican, I know what authentic Mexican food should taste like), but the margaritas are great along with other drinks. The decor and atmosphere is very fun and young. They have an upstairs and downstairs area, both with outside patios. Located right off the Venice Beach Boardwalk, it is the perfect location for "drinks on the beach" (you can't literally drink on the beach, unfortunately, but you catch my flow).

Taco Tuesday was great! I was worried about trying the tacos but once they were on the table I was excited to try them! Not disapointed at all; they were really delicious, at least the steak and chicken ones I had were. They had plenty of meat and came with a side of mexican rice and black beans. Paired up with a giant margarita, Taco Tuesday was perfect here! It was a full house for the Happy Hour which goes from 4pm-10pm, everyone enjoying a conversation over sports, food, and drinks.

Since it gets really busy, service isn't as quick but thats understandable. All the servers are very nice. I've never had a issue with customer service here. Parking sucks, but if you are lucky you might just get a meter right outside or there is also valet across the street and a parking lot at the end of the street.< /text>< Pictures>
None< /Pictures>

<name>terry bledsoe<//name><time>1476129340707< /time>< rating>
1< /rating>
< Review>
I barely write reviews because I dnt wanna take the time to talk about a place unless it really deserves it. I have never been to a place that treats you with such disrespect. This cabo cantina needs to take some pointers from the other locations like the one in West Hollywood.  I get it it's like the "Mexican style" bar and grill so you don't expect much. But you should at least be treated like a customer. First the blended Mega Margarita that I split with my friends was really icy. It taste like a slurpee from 7 11 that was really watered down. Way to much ice. I coulnt even taste the flavor I got let alone the alcohol. But I drank it anyway. Didn't bother to tell the server. We also got nachos which was great. Then I ordered buy one get one Margarita on ice which was really good. The problem didn't really come until we got the bill. The server (I dnt know her name but seems to be a dark hair white girl)  wrote 20% of 100 =$20 on the ticket. I'm a server my friends are servers so we felt really disrespected at the fact that she wrote it on the bill. Like we were going to do it anyway because we are of the industry but she didn't have to write it on the bill. We felt because we are a diverse group of minorities she had a need to write it on the bill. Some restaurants have the percentages PRINTED at the bottom for your convenience, but she flat out wrote it with her pen. When we asked her about it she brushed it off and said it was a bad habit. So then we start to wonder if this is policy so we called a manager( a seemingly white male named Guy )over. Before he came I saw her debrief him of what happen (which was really nothing). When he came he seem to already know what he was gonna say. When we asked him if it's policy he said yes because we have a lot of tourists come here. Then I said tourist are not you shouldn't try to force tip out of pple. Then he said its policy and its not going to change. And then said every cabo cantina is different.  I thought to myself yes every one is different, they aren't racist. The manager NAMED GUY was very rude. When I asked him for his name he said it was Guy and then he asked for mine and I said no. Which seem to really piss him off. It then Looked like he gestured to security to kick us out. They didn't get a chance to we were leaving anyway. My thing is you never know who you are going to get we were going to tip 20% anyway. Because of the manager we tipped her NOTHING. She wasnt a good server anyway. The team is only as good as the leader and the leader sucks. Not coming here again. I'll stick to what I know.< /Review>

< review>
I barely write reviews because I dnt wanna take the time to talk about a place unless it really deserves it. I have never been to a place that treats you with such disrespect. This cabo cantina needs to take some pointers from the other locations like the one in West Hollywood.  I get it it's like the "Mexican style" bar and grill so you don't expect much. But you should at least be treated like a customer. First the blended Mega Margarita that I split with my friends was really icy. It taste like a slurpee from 7 11 that was really watered down. Way to much ice. I coulnt even taste the flavor I got let alone the alcohol. But I drank it anyway. Didn't bother to tell the server. We also got nachos which was great. Then I ordered buy one get one Margarita on ice which was really good. The problem didn't really come until we got the bill. The server (I dnt know her name but seems to be a dark hair white girl)  wrote 20% of 100 =$20 on the ticket. I'm a server my friends are servers so we felt really disrespected at the fact that she wrote it on the bill. Like we were going to do it anyway because we are of the industry but she didn't have to write it on the bill. We felt because we are a diverse group of minorities she had a need to write it on the bill. Some restaurants have the percentages PRINTED at the bottom for your convenience, but she flat out wrote it with her pen. When we asked her about it she brushed it off and said it was a bad habit. So then we start to wonder if this is policy so we called a manager( a seemingly white male named Guy )over. Before he came I saw her debrief him of what happen (which was really nothing). When he came he seem to already know what he was gonna say. When we asked him if it's policy he said yes because we have a lot of tourists come here. Then I said tourist are not you shouldn't try to force tip out of pple. Then he said its policy and its not going to change. And then said every cabo cantina is different.  I thought to myself yes every one is different, they aren't racist. The manager NAMED GUY was very rude. When I asked him for his name he said it was Guy and then he asked for mine and I said no. Which seem to really piss him off. It then Looked like he gestured to security to kick us out. They didn't get a chance to we were leaving anyway. My thing is you never know who you are going to get we were going to tip 20% anyway. Because of the manager we tipped her NOTHING. She wasnt a good server anyway. The team is only as good as the leader and the leader sucks. Not coming here again. I'll stick to what I know.< /review>

Went here Monday and saw Tuesday they had charged my card 4 times, totaling an amount of over $120. When I called and asked what happened, the guy told me that they charge everyones cards before they close their tab, then charge the real amount. Well, I got charged 4 times when I should have been charged just twice, the guy told me to wait a couple days and if it doesnt go back to the card to call again. Well its saturday and its still there! so for people who dont check theyre statements you should after coming to this place. My friends and coworkers are never coming here again and we work in a restaurant! I cant even imagine how many people are screwed over by this, they dont even tell you before they do it and hope you dont notice the extra money in their pocket. Thanks to them I missed a bill and now I owe even more money because they wouldnt transfer the money back in time.
THANKS CABO YOURE NOT WORTH IT. The Whaler next store is way cleaner and they dont charge you ILLEGAL charges, which they should at least tell you in advance!!< /Review>
